msg:The hotel is very well located, right next to the lake and not far from Hanling village. We originally booked a garden view room but we were upgraded to a lake view. We had a terrace and the view was amazing!!! The compound is quite large and great for an evening stroll. 

The breakfast options were varied and the food was delicious. The restaurant staff were friendly and very attentive, and the overall atmosphere was relaxed and enjoyable. 

The staff at reception were also great. Very friendly when we arrived and very helpful to get us a golf cart to get to and from our room to the restaurant building.

The only small thing that could be improved in my opinion is the cleanliness in the room. I'm a bit of a clean freak so I noticed a few things that required attention: a small stain on the sofa, some stains on the toilet floor, and there was a small start of mpuld behind the sink taps. I would've also liked for the bins to have rubbish bags inside. Small things though, and overall we really enjoyed our stay, and we definitely return.

excellent: the food and beverage manager and restaurant staff were always friendly and the food was excellent (though I think the price of a beverages is outrageous). the Thai curry is highly recommended.

the pools and spa pools are great

the room is nice and the whole building is beautiful.

a birthday cake and card to celebrate was very special and thoughtful.

to improve:
the cocktails we're awful each time we tried a new one...the ingredients were listed but not all present in the drink

the check in and checkout - first and last impressions need to be improved. check in we didn't receive a friendly smile to guide us to the counter, check out was a long queue

during the busy time, more shuttle cars are required, we had several 20-30minutes wait times and guests act a bit silly and selfish, pushing to get on the shuttle bus even when families with small children where waiting longer. it was 40degrees Celsius so walking was not a safe option.

I had to call three times to get housekeeping on the first day and was told usually housekeeping only come every second day, which doesn't make sense. I don't need my bed made or towels changed, but I do need the trash removed daily. a bit of a strange policy for a pretty expensive hotel.

the play are for kids is nice and the staff are generally friendly and patient.

very mixed review I'm afraid.

msg:Sure, it is a stunning resort and overall we enjoyed the experience. However it is far from perfect. A few issues to consider:
1) I booked a deluxe room and relying on the picture I was expecting a sofa bed on the balcony. There was no sofa bed! Bummer. 
2) The bathtub is quite small, mostly for one person. 
3) The guest rooms feel/are quite distant from the lake. The view is so so. 
4) The resort is not really on the lake, there is a road separating it from the lake. so no rooms or villa really on the lake.
5) They mention a shuttle bus to nearby Hanling old street, but it was only running every 2 hours and needed booking... a bit complicated for a 4 minute ride. 
6) The main building with the lobby has very limited facilities. Just a small deck for outdoor dining. 
Overall ok, recommend to book on a weekday when the price is cheaper. I give 5 for service because it was a busy weekend and personnel was all very professional and efficient, but I did not experience anything exceptional. I tried the high end Chinese restaurant that was good and also the breakfast in line with a 5 star hotel.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Garden-view Double Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 20, 2024
msg:I stayed at Cordis for three days and one night, and I was generally very satisfied. At first, I was struggling between Cordis, Huaqiao Howard Johnson, Boyue and Qianhu State Guesthouse. The four hotels can be said to have their own characteristics and activities. Cordis has large rooms, good views, and a children's playground. Huaqiao Howard Johnson has private hot springs and naughty castles. Boyue has a high-end style. Qianhu State Guesthouse has the legendary Qianhu Secret Realm Train (but in fact, it is said to be just a very ordinary children's train, and it is too old school). After comprehensive consideration, I still chose Cordis. Facts have proved that choosing Cordis is still wise.

Environment:
Whether it is greening, view, orientation, or distance to the Shangshui Campground, it is unique, and I also like the hotel fragrance. Dongyue Market has outdoor tables and chairs, and there are several white swans on the lawn next to it, which makes our children very happy. The biggest disadvantage is that you need to take a shuttle bus from the guest room to other areas. This point can also be said to be complementary, because the room is large and independent. Being in the same building, without having to walk around, the room and view are bound to be not so good, so I can accept it. Moreover, the shuttle bus also responded very promptly, so the travel was not affected at all.

Service:
Whether it is the guest room, front desk, lobby, or concierge, everyone responded very quickly and responded to every request, especially the duty manager Andy. When I checked in, I added WeChat and any matter would be replied and solved in the first time, which was very satisfactory. At first, I was worried that some reviews said that there would be charges for bottled water beyond the free quota, so I brought a large bucket of water with me, but later I found that it was unnecessary. Just ask them for room service, and they give it very quickly.

Dining:
As for Ming Court, I feel that if I have the opportunity to make a separate appoin**ent for dinner in Shanghai, it is not necessary to go to the hotel. The buffet at Dongyue Market is very nice. The selection is complete, the taste is fusion, and there are many dishes suitable for babies. Em... The coffee machine only has espresso and ameicano, and the others are provided by on-site service. Although the latte art is beautiful and the lady is very fast, I always feel that the supply is insufficient to meet the demand. The afternoon tea in the lobby bar, em... is just average, the focus is on appearance, the taste... em... why not consider asking the chef of Dongyue Market to make afternoon tea together?

Hygiene:
Overall it is OK, the details need to be improved. Or, I can think of it as being near the lake and the wind is strong, it is indeed easier to accumulate dust than hotels in the city center, and because of this, cleaning needs to be more careful. However, it is not as terrible as the bad reviews say. I carefully looked through every corner and there are not as many mold spots as imagined, so I can still stay at ease.

Baby bed:
The most humane one in the hotel I have stayed in, wide enough and canvas, which can meet the needs of babies of all ages. This one needs to be given a hundred stars!

Actually, there were some episodes before check-in. The children's playground was closed before the end of June, which made us very depressed. My friend and I made an appoin**ent to meet at Dongqian Lake in Ningbo. Both of us brought our children. It was really bad that there was no children's playground, but the hotel still gave as many solutions as possible. And it turned out that although there was no children's playground, the children could enjoy more outdoor time. We chose the Shangshui camping site, played football on the lawn, and watched the swans by the small bridge. The day passed quickly. Moreover, the duty manager and Ctrip's customer service were also very awesome. In fact, before the refund and change, I also saw that the group purchase on ** was newer and more favorable than Ctrip, but considering that various demands needed to be mediated, I still wanted to use Ctrip's customer service, so I didn't switch in the end. It turns out that a little price difference is still worth it. But, we still hope that the children's playground can be opened as soon as possible, and we will not be disappointed next time we stay~~~ (I am really unlucky. I went to two cities in two consecutive months. The hotels I chose were all closed for renovations a week before departure. What kind of evil is this...)

Finally, I still need to highlight Andy. He has the level of a first-class hotel. Anyway, compared with my experience at Shangri-La Qiantan in Shanghai, Dongqian Lake CORDIS is better. Moreover, Andy has a smile that should be in the service industry to customers, which makes people feel at home quickly. Praise!

It is more than one kilometer to Hanling Old Street. When the weather is good, you can take a walk along the lake. Parking near the old street is difficult on weekends, so walking is really the best option. After dinner, it was time to take a walk back to the hotel.
The breakfast is average, but the basics are available. The restaurant is large and there are seats no matter how crowded it is. It would be better if there were a few changes every day.
After all, it is a courtyard-style hotel with a lot of green plants, so there are still many blind spots for hygiene. I hope the room cleaning can be more detailed.
There are two swimming lanes in the hotel swimming pool. There are not many people and it is very comfortable to swim. However, the changing room is a bit small.
Dongqian Lake has infinite scenery, and overall it was a very satisfying trip.

The light pink carpet under the bed is very dirty, so it's very low.

Swimming pool: The swimming pool and hot water bubble pool in the health center are very good and there is no one. Unfortunately, we did not bring a swimsuit and did not use it. The service staff was particularly enthusiastic to take us around

Transportation: The hotel is very big, you can call a buggy when you go out and you need to wait five minutes. There is a shuttle bus to Dongqianhu Metro Station every two hours

I encountered an episode when I took a bath at night and found that there was no hot water. Two staff members came before and after. Later, it was found that both boilers were broken. One hour later, one was repaired, but the temperature was still not too high and the water pressure was not enough.

The overall feeling is good, the service is also ok, the architecture and landscape are quite good, will consider again

The first time I stayed in a hotel, I was stranded in the lobby for half an hour to get back to my room.
